造谣生事
造谣生事，诬蔑他人。
竭尽造谣诬蔑之能事
jiéjìn zàoyáo wūmiè zhī néngshì 
stop at nothing in spreading lies and slanders
纯粹是无中生有，当面造谣。
Chúncuì shì wú zhōng shēngyǒu，dāngmiàn zàoyáo。
Nothing but rumours fabricated out of thin air and brazen lies.
你血口喷人，纯粹是造谣！
nǐ xuèkǒupēnrén，chúncuì shì zàoyáo！
You\'re slinging mud at me—that\'s a pack of lies!
制造谣言
zhìzào yáoyán 
fabricate rumours (or lies)
造谣惑众
zàoyáo huòzhòng
fabricate rumours to mislead people
造谣
zàoyáo
cook up a story and spread it around; start a rumour
你不但没有意识到自己的错误，反而造谣惑众！
Nǐ búdàn méiyǒu yìshídào zìjǐ de cuòwù，fǎnér zàoyáo huòzhòng！
Not only did you not realize your own mistakes, but also fabricated rumours that mislead other people.

这个歹徒太手黑了，把他的骨头都打折了。
Zhège dǎitú tài shǒuhēi le，bǎ tā de gǔtou dōu dǎshé le。
This bandit was so cruel, he broke the man\'s bones.
心狠手辣是这伙儿歹徒的一贯特点，我们一定要尽快破案，减少受害者的数量。
Xīnhěn shǒulà shì zhè huǒr dǎitú de yíguàn tèdiǎn，wǒmen yídìng yào jìnkuài pòàn，jiǎnshǎo shòuhàizhě de shùliàng。
Extreme cruelty and lack of mercy have always been these gangsters\' characteristics. We must crack the case as soon as possible so as to reduce the number of sufferers.
面对歹徒，他总能表现出泰然自若的神情，充分体现出一位老刑警的冷静与睿智。
Miànduì dǎitú，tā zǒng néng biǎoxiàn chū tàiránzìruò de shénqíng，chōngfèn tǐxiàn chū yíwèi lǎoxíngjǐng de lěngjìng yǔ ruìzhì。
He is calm and fearless when faced with a gangster, displaying the soberness and wisdom of a long-time criminal policeman.
这群歹徒心黑手辣，什么事都做得出来。
Zhè qún dǎitú xīnhēi shǒulà，shénme shì dōu zuò de chūlái。
These gangsters are cold-blooded and capable of doing anything.
歹徒目露凶光的样子让她很害怕。
Dǎitú mùlòu xiōngguāng de yàngzi ràng tā hěn hàipà。
The ferocious look in the gangster\'s eyes scared her very much.
歹徒的凶蛮相是无论如何也吓不倒我们的。
Dǎitú de xiōngmán xiàng shì wúlùn rúhé yě xiàbùdǎo wǒmen de。
Gangsters can never threaten us by their cruelty.
面对凶顽的歹徒，勇敢的民警毫不畏惧。
Miànduì xiōngwán de dǎitú，yǒnggǎn de mínjǐng háobú wèijù。
Facing the dangerous gangsters, the brave policemen were not frightened at all.
这个歹徒贼头贼脑的，寻机作案。
Zhège dǎitú zéitóu zéinǎo de，xúnjī zuòàn。
This thief behaves stealthily and looks for an opportunity to steal something.
干警缴获了歹徒用来行凶的折刀。
Gànjǐng jiǎohuò le dǎitú yònglái xíngxiōng de zhédāo。
The policmen seized the folding knife that was used by the scoundrels.
疯狂的歹徒以自爆结束了他罪恶的生命。
Fēngkuáng de dǎitú yǐ zìbào jiéshù le tā zuìè de shēngmìng。
The crazy bandit attempted to end his evil life with a suicide bomb.
歹徒手持自动步枪绑架人质，被公安干警拿下。
Dǎitú shǒuchí zìdòng bùqiāng bǎngjià rénzhì，bèi gōng\'ān gànjǐng náxià。
The bandit who kidnapped the hostage with an automatic rifle was seized by police.
我们面对的是罪恶滔天的歹徒，所以在对决时不能有半点犹豫。
Wǒmen miànduì de shì zuìè tāotiān de dǎitú，suǒyǐ zài duìjué shí bùnéng yǒu bàndiǎn yóuyù。
In front of us are the most heinous criminals, so we shouldn\'t hesitate at all when confronting them.
她终于逃出了歹徒的魔掌。
Tā zhōngyú táochūle dǎitú de mózhǎng.
She finally escaped from the clutches of the thugs.
歹徒见她要拼命转身跑掉了。
Dǎitú jiàn tā yào pīnmìng zhuǎnshēn pǎo diàole.
When the thugs saw that she was ready to fight to the death, they turned and fled.

The gunman, now in police custody, is repentant.

The couple were shot when three gunmen hijacked their car, even though they did not resist.

&quot;Red&quot; is an attributive adjective in &quot;a red apple&quot;.
“Red（hóngsè de）”zài“a red apple（yí gè hóng píngguǒ）”zhōng shì yí gè zuò dìngyǔ de xíngróngcí。
“red（红色的）”在“a red apple（一个红苹果）”中是一个做定语的形容词。
&quot;Red&quot; is a predicative adjective in &quot;the apple is red&quot;.
Zài“zhège píngguǒ shì hóngsè de”zhè jù huà zhōng，“hóngsè de”shì biǎoyǔ xíngróngcí。
在“这个苹果是红色的”这句话中，“红色的”是表语形容词。
